<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wren.html>wren</a> (120591)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">wrenne</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">wranne</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">wrenna</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">wrænna</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">werna</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">wærna</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">wrenne</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:wren.html>wren</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wrandijô</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:wren.html>wren</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">wrendilo</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:wren.html>wren</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">rento</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">rentilo</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:wren.html>wren</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">rindel</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:wren.html>wren</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is">rindill</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:wren.html>wren</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:wren.html>wren</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">wrens</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Any member of a mainly New World passerine bird family Troglodytidae; <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/true_wren" class="extiw" title="w:true wren">true <a href = vnd.unilang:wren.html>wren</a></a>.
<ol><li><i>Troglodytes troglodytes</i> (Eurasian <a href = vnd.unilang:wren.html>wren</a>)</li></ol></li>
<li>Small bird of similar appearance to a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/true_wren" class="extiw" title="w:true wren">true <a href = vnd.unilang:wren.html>wren</a></a>.</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wrikken.html>wrikken</a> (33648)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Ultimately from  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wrigōną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to wriggle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*wreyḱ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to turn, wrap, tie</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*wer-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to turn, bend</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Perhaps related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">wriggen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to twist</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wrikken.html>wrikken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to pry, wrench</li></ol>

***wroeging.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wroeging.html>wroeging</a> (17265)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">wroegen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to blame, to accuse</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wroeging.html>wroeging</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wroeging.html>wroegingen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wroeging.html>wroeginkje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>repentance, remorse</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:wroeging.html>wroeging</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span> <sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:spijt.html>spijt</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:gewetensnood.html>gewetensnood</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:berouw.html>berouw</a>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:wroeten.html>wroeten</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*wruotan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wrōtaną</i>.

***wulf.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wulf.html>wulf</a> (58493)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wulfaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*wĺ̥kʷos</i>. Germanic cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Frisian" class="extiw" title="w:Old Frisian">Old Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ofs"><a href = vnd.unilang:wolf.html>wolf</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx"><a href = vnd.unilang:wulf.html>wulf</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:wulf.html>wulf</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh"><a href = vnd.unilang:wolf.html>wolf</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">úlfr</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gothic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gothic language">Gothic</a></span> <i class="Goth mention" lang="got">𐍅𐌿𐌻𐍆𐍃</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">wulfs</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The Indo-European root <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> also the source of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Avestan" class="extiw" title="w:Avestan">Avestan</a></span> <i class="Avst mention" lang="ae">𐬬𐬆𐬵𐬭𐬐𐬀</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ae-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vəhrka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">vilkas</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">влькъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vlĭkŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">λύκος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lúkos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">lupus</i> also probably from the same root, either internally borrowed or with metathesis because of a <a href = vnd.unilang:wolf.html>wolf</a> taboo.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latinx headword" lang="ang"><a href = vnd.unilang:wulf.html>wulf</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:wolf.html>wolf</a>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latinx mention e-example" lang="ang"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:wulf.html>Wulf</a></b> āna mæġ <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wulf.html>wulf</a></b> ġefēhþ.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Only a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wolf.html>wolf</a></b> can catch a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wolf.html>wolf</a></b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wunderbar.html>wunderbar</a> (58492)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">wunderbære</i> (also <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">wunderberen</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">wunderberende</i>), equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Wunder</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">-bar</i>. Akin to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">German Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds-de">wunnerbaar</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">wunnerbor</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wonderbaar.html>wonderbaar</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Saterland_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Saterland Frisian language">Saterland Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="stq">wunderboar</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">underbar</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:wunderbar.html>wunderbar</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-de comparative-form-of" lang="de">wunderbarer</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-de superlative-form-of" lang="de">am wunderbarsten</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>wonderful</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wurgen.html>wurgen</a> (7828)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">worgen</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:wurgen.html>wurgen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:wurgen.html>wurgen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wurgijaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*werǵʰ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bind, squeeze</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">würgen</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">worry</i>.

<p>Probably borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:yeti.html>yeti</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Standard_Tibetan" class="extiw" title="w:Standard Tibetan">Tibetan</a></span> <i class="Tibt mention" lang="bo">གཡའ་དྲེད</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bo-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">g.ya' dred</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">rock bear</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, compound of <i class="Tibt mention" lang="bo">གཡའ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bo-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">g.ya'</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:rocky.html>rocky</a> or <a href = vnd.unilang:rocky.html>rocky</a> place</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Tibt mention" lang="bo">དྲེད</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bo-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dred</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bear</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***ying.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ying.html>ying</a> (22036)</h1><br></body> 
***yo-yo.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:yo-yo.html>yo-yo</a> (77933)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Formerly a trademark. Most likely from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ilocano_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ilocano language">Ilocano</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ilo">yóyo</i>, or another <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Philippine_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Philippine languages">Philippine</a></span> cognate. <span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:yo-yo.html>yo-yo</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">yo-yos</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A toy consisting of a spheroidal or cylindrical spindle having a circular groove in which string <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> wound; it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used by holding the string in the <a href = vnd.unilang:fingers.html>fingers</a> and reeling the spindle up and down by movements of the wrist.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms coordinate-term"><span class="defdate">Coordinate <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a>:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">diabolo</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">whirligig</span></span></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">I bought a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:yo-yo.html>yo-yo</a></b> from the toy store yesterday.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">finance</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A volatile market that <a href = vnd.unilang:moves.html>moves</a> up and down.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Someone who vacillates.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sewing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A cloth <a href = vnd.unilang:rosette.html>rosette</a> formed by gathering the outside edge of a circle of fabric in toward the centre using a running stitch.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A foolish, annoying or incompetent person.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> hard to watch the management for very long and not conclude that the place <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> run by a bunch of <b>yo-yos</b>.</i></div></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1985</b>,  Sting amp; Mark Knopfler (<a href = vnd.unilang:lyrics.html>lyrics</a> and music),  “Money for Nothing”, in  <cite>Brothers in Arms</cite>, performed by Dire Straits:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Now look at them <b>yo-yos</b>, that's the way you do it</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1991</b>,  Stephen King,  <cite>Needful <a href = vnd.unilang:things.html>Things</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:henry.html>Henry</a> glanced past him at the few other customers currently in attendance. "<a href = vnd.unilang:hey.html>Hey</a>! Any of you <b>yo-yos</b> headed up Castle Hill?"</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:yo-yo.html>yo-yo</a> dieting</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:yo-yo.html>yo-yo</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">yo-yos</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">yo-yoing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">yo-yoed</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To vacillate; to move up and down.
<ul><li><b>1990</b>, <i>The Economist</i> (volume 316, page 93)
<dl><dd>The <b>yo-yoing</b> stockmarket whizzed back up by around a quarter and then started to fall again.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
</body>

***yuck.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:yuck.html>yuck</a> (85878)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Unknown. Akin to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jak.html>jak</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">disgusting</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p><p><span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:yuck.html>yuck</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">Uttered to indicate disgust usually toward an objectionable taste or odour.</span> <span class="defdate">[from 1966]</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:yum.html>yum</a></span></span></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:yuck.html>Yuck</a></b>! This peanut butter <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> disgusting!</i></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li>See Thesaurus:<a href = vnd.unilang:yuck.html>yuck</a></li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">yucky</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:yuck.html>yuck</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">yucks</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Something disgusting.
<ul><li><b>2003</b>, <i>The New Yorker,</i> 8 Dec 2003
<dl><dd>I fetched an orange from a basket and peeled it <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> “Make sure you peel as much of the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:yuck.html>yuck</a></b> off as possible,” she <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a>. “I hate the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:yuck.html>yuck</a></b>."</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">countable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The sound made by a laugh.
<ul><li><b>2000</b>, <i>The New Yorker,</i> 13 March 2000
<dl><dd>Given this insecurity, the creators of “The Simpsons” <a href = vnd.unilang:took.html>took</a> an extraordinary risk: they decided not to use a laugh track. On almost all other <a href = vnd.unilang:sitcoms.html>sitcoms</a>, dialogue <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> interrupted repeatedly by crescendos of phony guffaws (or by the electronically enhanced laughter of live audiences), creating the unreal ebb and flow of sitcom conversation, in which a typical character’s initial reaction to an ostensibly humorous remark could only be to smile archly or look around while waiting for the <b>yucks</b> to <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> down.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">jucken</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jeuken.html>jeuken</a></i>, and see <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">itch</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:yuck.html>yuck</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">yucks</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">yucking</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">yucked</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To itch.
<dl><dd><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> find and add a quotation of Grose to this entry?)</span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***yup.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> yup (16045)</h1><br><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b>yup</b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>

<p>Originally an acronym for <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">young upwardly mobile professional</i> or <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">young urban professional</i>,  + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:-ie.html>-ie</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos">suffix forming noun signifying person associated with suffixed noun</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***zaad.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:zaad.html>zaad</a> (6638)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">saet</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*sāt</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*sēdiz</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds"><a href = vnd.unilang:saad.html>Saad</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Saat</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">sied</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">seed</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">sæd</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***zaaien.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:zaaien.html>zaaien</a> (9334)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">sâyen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*sāien</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*sēaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*seh₁-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zaaien.html>zaaien</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to sow, plant seed</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to start, set in motion
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verbod.html>verbod</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zaaien.html>zaaien</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:zaaide.html>zaaide</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:onrust.html>onrust</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:onder.html>onder</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:boeren.html>boeren</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The sowing ban <b>caused</b> unrest among the farmers.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***zaak.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:zaak.html>zaak</a> (416)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">sāke</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*saka</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*sakō</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">sake</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">saak</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cause; business</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">Saak</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Sache</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">thing; matter; cause; legal cause</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">sag</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norwegian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Norwegian language">Norwegian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="no"><a href = vnd.unilang:sak.html>sak</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gothic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gothic language">Gothic</a></span> <i class="Goth mention" lang="got">𐍃𐌰𐌺𐌾𐍉</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sakjō</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dispute, argument</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zaak.html>zaak</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zaken.html>zaken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zaakje.html>zaakje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:zaakwaarnemer.html>zaakwaarnemer</a> (34499)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zaak.html>zaak</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:waarnemer.html>waarnemer</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zaakwaarnemer.html>zaakwaarnemer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zaakwaarnemers.html>zaakwaarnemers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zaakwaarnemer.html>zaakwaarnemertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>

***zaal.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:zaal.html>zaal</a> (3427)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">sale</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">sala</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*saliz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zaal.html>zaal</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zalen.html>zalen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zaaltje.html>zaaltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>room, hall</li>
<li>ward in a hospital or similar medical or caregiving institute</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Germanic single-room home</li></ol>
